**12. Assessment Procedure**
- ⚠️ VERIFY — the 48-month time limit (up from the original 24 months under FA 2022) and the two additional 60%/70% slabs were introduced by a later Finance Act; confirm against the Finance Act applicable to your specific exam attempt, as this is one of the more recently amended provisions in the chapter.
- **Pitfalls / exam tips:** ⚠️ VERIFY — the ₹3,750–₹7,500/hour special-audit remuneration band is drawn from Income-tax Rule 14B; confirm the current Rule 14B figures haven't been revised for the exam year, as fee-slab rules are periodically updated by notification.
- ⚠️ VERIFY — the Sec 158BFA(1) interest rate of **1.5% per month** should be cross-checked against the bare Act/latest CBDT clarification for your exact exam attempt; the historical (pre-2003) block-assessment interest rate under this section was aligned to the Sec 234A rate of 1% per month, and this chapter's reintroduction via FA 2024 is one of the newest provisions in the syllabus.

**13. Appeals, Revisions & Dispute Resolution Committee**
- ⚠️ VERIFY — the OCR cites *Pepsi Foods Ltd. (2021)* as a **Supreme Court** ruling; the landmark judgment reading down the third proviso to Sec 254(2A) (striking the automatic vacation of stay where delay is *not* attributable to the assessee) is generally attributed to the **Delhi High Court (2015)**, later followed/affirmed in subsequent rulings — confirm the exact forum/year before quoting in an answer.

**14. Miscellaneous Provisions, Penalties, Prosecutions & The Black Money Act, 2015**
- **Sec. 273A — Waiver/reduction of penalty by PCIT/CIT:** conditions — voluntary & full disclosure in good faith before detection, co-operation in enquiry, and payment of tax + interest in full. Relief available **only once in the assessee's lifetime**. ⚠️ VERIFY — OCR states CIT/PCIT can waive without higher approval where income is up to ₹5 lakh, and needs CCIT/PCCIT/DGIT approval above ₹5 lakh; this appears to be an administrative/circular-based monetary limit rather than a figure appearing in bare Sec. 273A text — confirm current CBDT instruction figure before quoting in an exam answer.

**15. GAAR, Taxation of VDA & Exempt Income**
- ⚠️ VERIFY — OCR groups this content under a single "Sec 96" heading; per the Income-tax Act, the IAA definition is Sec 96 and the deemed-lack-of-commercial-substance rules are a **separate Sec 97** — treated separately above for accuracy.
- 2. PC/C issues a notice to the assessee to submit objections/be heard within a specified period — ⚠️ VERIFY: the OCR states "not exceeding 60 days"; the statutory language in Sec 144BA is commonly cited as a **60-day** period for the assessee to respond — confirm the exact wording ("not less than"/fixed 60 days) against the bare Act before using it in a written answer.
- ⚠️ VERIFY — the case citation in source material ("Kribhco (2012)(Delhi)" — that Sec 14A applies only to income exempt under Chapter III) could not be independently confirmed this session; treat the **principle** (Sec 14A ≠ Chapter VI-A deductions) as settled law, but verify the exact case name/citation before quoting it in an answer.

**16. Tonnage Taxation, Taxation of Trust & Institutions, Tax Audit & Ethical Compliance**
- ⚠️ VERIFY — Finance Act 2025 amendment (w.e.f. 1.4.2025): where a trust's total income (before Sec. 11/12 exemption) does **not exceed ₹5 crore** in each of the two P.Y.s preceding the year of application, registration/approval (other than provisional) is valid for **10 years instead of 5 years**. Cross-check the exact ₹5 crore threshold and effective date against the Finance Act 2025 text/CBDT notification before quoting in the exam.
- Explanation 3A: donations for repair/renovation of a temple/mosque/gurdwara/church notified u/s 80G(2)(b) may be treated as corpus donation if used only for repair/renovation, not further donated, kept separately identifiable, and invested per Sec. 11(5) — ⚠️ VERIFY the "FA 22 / w.e.f. AY 21-22" tag in the source; the AY precedes the cited Finance Act, which is internally inconsistent — cross-check against the actual Finance Act (likely FA 2023).
- ⚠️ VERIFY — the source states MMR = **34.944% (30% + 12% surcharge + 4% cess)**. This matches the MMR structure applicable when the highest AOP/individual surcharge slab was 12% (broadly, pre-FY2016-17 rates). Under the surcharge slabs in force for several recent Finance Acts (10%/15%/25%/37% based on income slabs, with 37% for income >₹5 crore), the MMR commonly used for AOP/trust taxation (and hence Sec. 115TD) computes to **30% + 37% + 4% cess ≈ 42.744%**. Confirm the MMR percentage applicable for the relevant P.Y. against the current Finance Act's Part I / Part III rate schedule before using either figure in an exam answer.

**17. Transfer Pricing**
- ⚠️ VERIFY — the foreign-currency benchmark is prescribed in Rule 10CB as "6-month LIBOR"; since LIBOR has been globally discontinued (USD LIBOR ceased mid-2023), confirm whether CBDT has since notified a replacement reference rate (e.g., a SOFR/ARR-based rate) for the relevant assessment year before relying on this in a foreign-currency numerical.
- ⚠️ VERIFY — **Notification No. 10/2025** (excluding IFSC finance companies from Sec. 94B) is a recent notification; confirm its exact number/date and conditions (no public deposits accepted, not registered as a Banking Unit, restricted to permissible IFSC treasury/lending/factoring activities, and borrowing in foreign currency) against the CBDT notification in force for the AY being examined.

**20. Application & Interpretation of Tax Treaties, BEPS & Latest Developments in International Taxation**
- ⚠️ VERIFY — The Supreme Court, in *Assessing Officer (IT) v. Nestlé SA* (12 Oct 2023), upheld that a sec. 90(1) notification is a **mandatory pre-condition** for MFN benefit to apply under domestic law, and that "OECD membership" for condition (2) is tested **at the time of signing** the second treaty (not merely at any later date) — reversing the taxpayer-favourable Delhi HC view (Concentrix/Nestlé). Students should quote this ruling as the current settled law for CA Final 2026.
- | 4 | Limit interest deductions/thin capitalisation — Fixed Ratio Rule (interest capped at a % of EBITDA), Group Ratio Rule, targeted rules for banks/insurers | **Sec. 94B** — restricts interest deduction to **30% of EBITDA** on interest paid/payable to an associated enterprise, applicable only where interest expenditure exceeds ⚠️ VERIFY — **₹1 crore**; excess disallowed can be carried forward 8 assessment years; banking/insurance business excluded |
- | 6 | Prevent treaty abuse/treaty shopping — Preamble statement (treaty not for non-taxation via shopping), **LOB** (objective tests — legal form, ownership, activity, expenditure) and **PPT** (principal purpose test, a GAAR-type rule) | LOB example: India–Mauritius Protocol (2016) shell/conduit test — total operational expenditure below the prescribed threshold in the preceding 12 months denies treaty benefit; ⚠️ VERIFY — threshold is commonly cited as **₹27,00,000** (or MUR 15,00,000), not the ₹7,00,000 figure in some source notes |
- ⚠️ VERIFY — As of the 2026 CA Final syllabus cut-off, India has **not yet enacted** domestic GloBE/QDMTT legislation; questions are expected to remain conceptual/OECD-framework based unless a Finance Act amendment is notified before the attempt.

**21. Foreign Tax Credit Rule, Conversion of Foreign Income & Remaining Case Laws**
- | **Frontier Information Tech Ltd. (Telangana HC)** ⚠️ VERIFY — exact citation/year not legible in source | Conversion of unpaid interest into **equity shares** amounts to "actual payment" u/s 43B — issuing shares discharges/extinguishes the interest liability, so it is not a mere book entry; deduction u/s 43B is allowable in the year of such conversion. (Consistent with the Supreme Court's reasoning in *M.M. Aqua Technologies* on conversion of interest into debentures.) |
- ### 7. Recent CBDT Circulars & Notifications ⚠️ VERIFY — figures per source concept-book; cross-check against the live CBDT circular/notification text before the exam
- **(f) Contract R&D relating to software development, or to generic pharmaceutical drugs:** minimum OP/OpEx **24%**, ⚠️ VERIFY — where transaction value is up to ₹300 crore (source states ₹300 crore; some editions of Rule 10TD list this ceiling at ₹200 crore — confirm the currently notified figure before the exam).
